 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Australia"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="640">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a></b>&nbsp;– Commonwealth of Australia </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Australia is a <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realm</a><sup id="cite_ref-realm_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-realm-7">[e]</a></sup> and a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of both <a href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_Australia" title="States and territories of Australia">states and territories</a>. There are six states, three internal territories, six external territories and one <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">claimed</a> Antarctic external territory. The external territories of Australia are: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Ashmore_and_Cartier_Islands" title="Ashmore and Cartier Islands">Ashmore and Cartier Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg/23px-Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg/35px-Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg/46px-Flag_of_Christmas_Island.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Christmas_Island" title="Christmas Island">Christmas Island</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Cocos_%28Keeling%29_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cocos_(Keeling)_Islands" title="Cocos (Keeling) Islands">Cocos (Keeling) Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Coral_Sea_Islands_Territory" class="mw-redirect" title="Coral Sea Islands Territory">Coral Sea Islands Territory</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Heard_Island_and_McDonald_Islands" title="Heard Island and McDonald Islands">Heard Island and McDonald Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg/23px-Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg/35px-Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg/46px-Flag_of_Norfolk_Island.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="920" data-file-height="460">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Island" title="Norfolk Island">Norfolk Island</a></li> 
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Australian_Antarctic_Territory" title="Australian Antarctic Territory">Australian Antarctic Territory</a></i></li>
  </ul> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_China#International_recognition_of_the_People's_Republic_of_China" title="Foreign relations of China">Partially unrecognised</a>. <span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> </span>Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">China contains five autonomous regions, <a href="/wiki/Guangxi" title="Guangxi">Guangxi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ningxia" title="Ningxia">Ningxia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region" title="Tibet Autonomous Region">Tibet</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-autonomous_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autonomous-9">[f]</a></sup> Additionally, it has sovereignty over the <a href="/wiki/Special_administrative_regions_of_China" title="Special administrative regions of China">Special Administrative Regions</a> of: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/23px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/35px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/45px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/45px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a></li>
  </ul> <p>China claims, but does not control <a href="#Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, which is governed by a rival administration (the Republic of China) that claims all of China as its territory.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-24">[m]</a></sup> </p><p>China is not recognised by <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_China#Countries_that_have_no_diplomatic_relations_with_the_PRC" title="Foreign relations of China">15</a> UN member states and <a href="/wiki/Vatican_City" title="Vatican City">Vatican City</a>, which, with the exception of Bhutan, all recognise Taiwan instead.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[n]</a></sup> </p> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Denmark"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/20px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/31px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/40px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="387">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a></b>&nbsp;– Kingdom of Denmark </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Member of the EU.<sup id="cite_ref-EU_4-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EU-4">[c]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Denmark" class="mw-redirect" title="Kingdom of Denmark">Kingdom of Denmark</a> includes 2 self-governing territories: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/21px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/32px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/41px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands" title="Faroe Islands">Faroe Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/45px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a></li>
  </ul> <p>The continental territory of Denmark, the Faroe Islands, and Greenland form the three constituent countries of the Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[s]</a></sup> The Kingdom of Denmark as a whole is a member of the EU, but EU law <a href="/wiki/Greenland_Treaty" class="mw-redirect" title="Greenland Treaty">does not apply</a> to the Faroe Islands and Greenland.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[15]</a></sup> </p> </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Israel"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a></b>&nbsp;– State of Israel </td>

 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Israel" title="International recognition of Israel">Partially unrecognised</a> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Israel exerts strong control over the territory claimed by <a href="#Palestine">Palestine</a>. Israel annexed <a href="/wiki/East_Jerusalem" title="East Jerusalem">East Jerusalem</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[25]</a></sup> an annexation not recognised by the international community.<sup id="cite_ref-dis_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dis-52">[26]</a></sup> Israel maintains <a href="/wiki/West_Bank_Areas_in_the_Oslo_II_Accord" title="West Bank Areas in the Oslo II Accord">varying levels of control</a> over the rest of the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>, and although Israel no longer has a permanent civilian or military presence in the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a>, following its <a href="/wiki/Israel%27s_unilateral_disengagement_plan" class="mw-redirect" title="Israel's unilateral disengagement plan">unilateral disengagement</a>, it is still considered by some to be the occupying power under international law.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[27]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[28]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[29]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[31]</a></sup> <p>Israel is not recognised as a state by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Israel" title="International recognition of Israel">28 UN members</a> and the <a href="#SADR">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Palestine_Liberation_Organization" title="Palestine Liberation Organization">Palestine Liberation Organization</a>, which enjoys recognition by a majority of UN member states as the sole representative of the Palestinian people, also does not recognise Israel. </p> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Korea_North"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_North_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_North_Korea.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_North_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_North_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_North_Korea.svg/46px-Flag_of_North_Korea.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">Korea, North</a></b>&nbsp;– Democratic People's Republic of Korea </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">North Korea is not recognised by three UN members, <a href="#France">France</a>, <a href="#Japan">Japan</a>, and <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a>, the last of which claims to be the sole legitimate government of <a href="/wiki/Korea" title="Korea">Korea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[32]</a></sup> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Korea_South"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">Korea, South</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of Korea </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">South Korea has one autonomous region, <a href="/wiki/Jeju_Island" title="Jeju Island">Jejudo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-autonomous_9-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autonomous-9">[f]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[33]</a></sup> <p>South Korea is not recognised by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a>, which claims to be the sole legitimate government of <a href="/wiki/Korea" title="Korea">Korea</a>. </p> </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Netherlands"></span><b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="Netherlands"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span></b> – Kingdom of the Netherlands </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Member of the EU.<sup id="cite_ref-EU_4-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EU-4">[c]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> includes four areas with substantial autonomy: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/23px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/35px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/45px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Aruba" title="Aruba">Aruba</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaçao">Curaçao</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/45px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="675" data-file-height="450">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Sint_Maarten" title="Sint Maarten">Sint Maarten</a></li>
  </ul> <p>The continental part of the Netherlands, Aruba, Curaçao, and Sint Maarten form the four constituent countries of the Kingdom. Three other overseas territories (<a href="/wiki/Bonaire" title="Bonaire">Bonaire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saba" title="Saba">Saba</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sint_Eustatius" title="Sint Eustatius">Sint Eustatius</a>) are <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">special municipalities</a> of the continental Netherlands.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[ac]</a></sup> The Kingdom of the Netherlands as a whole is a member of the EU, but EU law applies only to parts within Europe. </p> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="New_Zealand"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/23px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/35px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/46px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a></b> </td>

 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">New Zealand is a <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-realm_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-realm-7">[e]</a></sup> and has one dependent territory and one <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">claimed</a> Antarctic dependent territory of: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Flag_of_Tokelau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Tokelau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Flag_of_Tokelau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Tokelau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Flag_of_Tokelau.svg/46px-Flag_of_Tokelau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="900">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Tokelau" title="Tokelau">Tokelau</a></li> 
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Ross_Dependency" title="Ross Dependency">Ross Dependency</a></i></li>
  </ul> <p>The <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Government" title="New Zealand Government">New Zealand Government</a> acts for the entire <a href="/wiki/Realm_of_New_Zealand" title="Realm of New Zealand">Realm of New Zealand</a> in all international contexts, which has responsibilities for (but no rights of control over) two freely <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">associated states</a>: </p> 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cook_Islands" title="Cook Islands">Cook Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/23px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/35px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/46px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Niue" title="Niue">Niue</a></li>
  </ul> <p>The Cook Islands and Niue have diplomatic relations with <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Cook_Islands" title="Foreign relations of the Cook Islands">49</a> and <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Niue" title="Foreign relations of Niue">18</a> UN members respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[34]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[35]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[36]</a></sup> They have full treaty-making capacity in the UN,<sup id="cite_ref-untreaty1_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-untreaty1-66">[37]</a></sup> and are members of some <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agencies</a>. </p> </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Norway"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/21px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/32px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/41px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="372">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a></b>&nbsp;– Kingdom of Norway </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Norway has two <a href="/wiki/Unincorporated_area" title="Unincorporated area">unincorporated areas</a> in Europe: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Svalbard" title="Svalbard">Svalbard</a> is an integral part of Norway, but has a special status due to the <a href="/wiki/Svalbard_Treaty" title="Svalbard Treaty">Svalbard Treaty</a>.</li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Jan_Mayen" title="Jan Mayen">Jan Mayen</a> is an uninhabited island that is an integral part of Norway, although unincorporated.</li>
  </ul> <p>Norway has one <a href="/wiki/Dependencies_of_Norway" title="Dependencies of Norway">dependent territory</a> and two <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">claimed</a> Antarctic dependent territories in the <a href="/wiki/Southern_Hemisphere" title="Southern Hemisphere">Southern Hemisphere</a>: </p> 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Bouvet_Island" title="Bouvet Island">Bouvet Island</a></li> 
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Peter_I_Island" title="Peter I Island">Peter I Island</a></i></li> 
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Queen_Maud_Land" title="Queen Maud Land">Queen Maud Land</a></i></li>
  </ul> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Oman"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/23px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/35px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/46px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a></b>&nbsp;– Sultanate of Oman </td>

<tr> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Pakistan"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/45px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a></b>&nbsp;– Islamic Republic of Pakistan </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Pakistan is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Subdivisions_of_Pakistan" class="mw-redirect" title="Subdivisions of Pakistan">four provinces and one capital territory</a>. Pakistan exercises control over certain portions of <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a>, but has not officially annexed any of it,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[38]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[39]</a></sup> instead regarding it as a disputed territory.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[40]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[41]</a></sup> The portions that it controls are divided into two territories, administered separately from Pakistan proper: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/23px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/35px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/45px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="648" data-file-height="432">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Azad_Kashmir" title="Azad Kashmir">Azad Kashmir</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/22px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="22" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/33px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/43px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1129" data-file-height="785">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Gilgit-Baltistan" title="Gilgit-Baltistan">Gilgit-Baltistan</a></li>
  </ul> <p>Azad Kashmir describes itself as a "self-governing state under Pakistani control", while Gilgit-Baltistan is described in its governance order as a group of "areas" with self-government.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[42]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com-73">[43]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AJ&amp;KHistory_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AJ&amp;KHistory-74">[44]</a></sup> These territories are not usually regarded as sovereign, as they do not fulfil the criteria set out by the declarative theory of statehood (for example, their current laws do not allow them to engage independently in relations with other states). Several state functions of these territories (such as foreign affairs and defence) are performed by Pakistan.<sup id="cite_ref-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com-73">[43]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[45]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[46]</a></sup> </p> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Palau"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of Palau </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Under <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> with the <a href="#United_States">United States</a>. </td>

<tr> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Palestine"></span><b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="Palestine"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a></span></b>&nbsp;– State of Palestine </td> 
 <td style="background:LightSkyBlue;"><span style="display:none">A</span> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">UN observer state</a>; member of 2 <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agencies</a> </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine">Partially unrecognised</a>. <span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> </span>Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The State of Palestine, declared in 1988, is not recognised as a state by Israel and has received diplomatic recognition from <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine">138</a> states.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[47]</a></sup> The proclaimed state has no agreed territorial borders, or effective control over much of the territory that it proclaimed.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[48]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian National Authority</a> is an interim administrative body formed as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Oslo_Accords" title="Oslo Accords">Oslo Accords</a> that exercises limited autonomous jurisdiction within the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_territories" title="Palestinian territories">Palestinian territories</a>. In foreign relations, Palestine is represented by the <a href="/wiki/Palestine_Liberation_Organization" title="Palestine Liberation Organization">Palestine Liberation Organization</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-unnms_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unnms-79">[49]</a></sup> The State of Palestine is a member state of UNESCO,<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[50]</a></sup> UNIDO and other international organizations.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[51]</a></sup> </td>
</tr>

Two, <a href="/wiki/Puntland" title="Puntland">Puntland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Galmudug" title="Galmudug">Galmudug</a>, have self-declared autonomy, while one, <a href="#Somaliland">Somaliland</a>, is <i>de facto</i> independent. </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="South_Sudan"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg/46px-Flag_of_South_Sudan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of South Sudan </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">South Sudan is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/wiki/States_of_South_Sudan" title="States of South Sudan">10 states and three administrative areas</a>. 
  <ul>
   <li>The <a href="/wiki/Abyei" title="Abyei">Abyei Area</a> is a zone with "special administrative status" established by the <a href="/wiki/Comprehensive_Peace_Agreement" title="Comprehensive Peace Agreement">Comprehensive Peace Agreement</a> in 2005. It is <i>de jure</i> a condominium of South Sudan and Sudan, but <i>de facto</i> administered by two competing administrations and the United Nations.<sup id="cite_ref-UNISFA2017_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNISFA2017-82">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AbyeiName_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbyeiName-83">[53]</a></sup></li>
  </ul> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The United Kingdom is a <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realm</a><sup id="cite_ref-realm_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-realm-7">[e]</a></sup> consisting of <a href="/wiki/Countries_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Countries of the United Kingdom">four constituent countries</a>; <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">Wales</a>. The United Kingdom has the following 13 <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">overseas territories</a> and one <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">claimed</a> Antarctic dependent territory:

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="United_States"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></b>&nbsp;– United States of America </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The United States is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Political_divisions_of_the_United_States#States_and_their_subdivisions" title="Political divisions of the United States">50 states</a>, one <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">federal district</a>, and one <a href="/wiki/Palmyra_Atoll" title="Palmyra Atoll">incorporated territory</a>. Additionally, the <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">Federal government of the United States</a> has sovereignty over 13 <a href="/wiki/Unincorporated_territories" class="mw-redirect" title="Unincorporated territories">unincorporated territories</a>. Of these territories, the following five are inhabited possessions: 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/23px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/35px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/46px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/American_Samoa" title="American Samoa">American Samoa</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/23px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/35px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/46px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="820" data-file-height="440">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="550">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/45px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1275" data-file-height="850">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">U.S. Virgin Islands</a></li>
  </ul> <p>It also has sovereignty over several uninhabited territories: </p> 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Baker_Island" title="Baker Island">Baker Island</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Howland_Island" title="Howland Island">Howland Island</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Jarvis_Island" title="Jarvis Island">Jarvis Island</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Johnston_Atoll" title="Johnston Atoll">Johnston Atoll</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingman_Reef" title="Kingman Reef">Kingman Reef</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Midway_Atoll" title="Midway Atoll">Midway Atoll</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Navassa_Island" title="Navassa Island">Navassa Island</a></li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a></li>
  </ul> <p>It also disputes sovereignty over the following two territories: </p> 
  <ul>
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Bajo_Nuevo_Bank" title="Bajo Nuevo Bank">Bajo Nuevo Bank</a></i></li> 
   <li><i><span class="flagicon" style="padding-left:25px;">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Serranilla_Bank" title="Serranilla Bank">Serranilla Bank</a></i></li>
  </ul> <p>Three sovereign states have become <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">associated states</a> of the United States under the <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a>: </p> 
  <ul>
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Marshall_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="570" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">Marshall Islands</a> – Republic of the Marshall Islands</li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="760" data-file-height="400">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Micronesia</a> – Federated States of Micronesia</li> 
   <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a> – Republic of Palau</li>
  </ul> </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Vatican_City"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg/16px-Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg/24px-Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg/32px-Flag_of_the_Vatican_City.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Vatican_City" title="Vatican City">Vatican City</a></b>&nbsp;– Vatican City State </td> 
 <td style="background:LightSkyBlue;"><span style="display:none">A</span> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">UN observer state</a> under the designation of "<a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>"; member of three <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agencies</a> and the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">IAEA</a> </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Administered by the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>, a sovereign entity with diplomatic relations to <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Holy_See" class="mw-redirect" title="International recognition of the Holy See">183&nbsp;states</a>. This figure consists of 180 UN member states, the Cook Islands, the Republic of China (Taiwan), and the State of Palestine.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[54]</a></sup> In addition, the European Union and the Sovereign Military Order of Malta maintain diplomatic relations with the Holy See. The Holy See is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">IAEA</a>, <a href="/wiki/International_Telecommunication_Union" title="International Telecommunication Union">ITU</a>, <a href="/wiki/Universal_Postal_Union" title="Universal Postal Union">UPU</a>, and <a href="/wiki/World_Intellectual_Property_Organization" title="World Intellectual Property Organization">WIPO</a> and a permanent observer of the UN (in the category of "Non-member State")<sup id="cite_ref-unnms_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unnms-79">[49]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Holy_See#Participation_in_international_organizations" title="Foreign relations of the Holy See">multiple other UN System organizations</a>. The Vatican City is governed by officials appointed by the <a href="/wiki/Pope" title="Pope">Pope</a>, who is the Bishop of the Diocese of Rome and <i><a href="/wiki/Ex_officio" class="mw-redirect" title="Ex officio">ex officio</a></i> sovereign of Vatican City. </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Cook_Islands"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Cook_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cook_Islands" title="Cook Islands">Cook Islands</a></b> </td> 
 <td style="background:lightgreen;"><span style="display:none">D</span> Member of eight <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agencies</a> </td> 
 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None<br><small>(See <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_the_Cook_Islands_and_Niue" title="Political status of the Cook Islands and Niue">political status</a>)</small> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A state in <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">free association</a> with <a href="#New_Zealand">New Zealand</a>, the Cook Islands maintains <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Cook_Islands" title="Foreign relations of the Cook Islands">diplomatic relations with&nbsp;52&nbsp;states</a>. The Cook Islands is a member of <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">multiple UN agencies</a> with full treaty making capacity.<sup id="cite_ref-untreaty1_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-untreaty1-66">[37]</a></sup> It shares a <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_New_Zealand" title="Monarchy of New Zealand">head of state</a> with New Zealand as well as having <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_nationality_law" title="New Zealand nationality law">shared citizenship</a>. </td>
</tr>
<tr> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Kosovo"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/21px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/32px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/42px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="840" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of Kosovo </td> 
 <td style="background:lightgreen;"><span style="display:none">D</span> Member of two <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agencies</a> </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Pursuant to <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1244" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1244">United Nations Security Council Resolution 1244</a>, Kosovo was placed under the administration of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Interim_Administration_Mission_in_Kosovo" title="United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo">United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo</a> in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[62]</a></sup> Kosovo <a href="/wiki/2008_Kosovo_declaration_of_independence" title="2008 Kosovo declaration of independence">declared independence in 2008</a>, and it has <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">received diplomatic recognition from&nbsp;113&nbsp;UN member states</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a>, while 18 states have recognized Kosovo only to later withdraw their recognition.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[63]</a></sup> Serbia continues to maintain its sovereignty claim over Kosovo. Other UN member states and non UN member states continue to recognise Serbian sovereignty or have taken no position on the question. Kosovo is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> and the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank_Group" title="World Bank Group">World Bank Group</a>. The Republic of Kosovo has <i>de facto</i> control over most of the territory, with limited control in <a href="/wiki/North_Kosovo" title="North Kosovo">North Kosovo</a>. </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Niue"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/23px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/35px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Niue.svg/46px-Flag_of_Niue.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Niue" title="Niue">Niue</a></b> </td>

 <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None<br><small>(See <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_the_Cook_Islands_and_Niue" title="Political status of the Cook Islands and Niue">political status</a>)</small> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A state in <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">free association</a> with <a href="#New_Zealand">New Zealand</a>, Niue maintains <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Niue" title="Foreign relations of Niue">diplomatic relations with&nbsp;20&nbsp;states</a>. Niue is a member of <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">multiple UN agencies</a> with full treaty making capacity.<sup id="cite_ref-untreaty1_66-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-untreaty1-66">[37]</a></sup> It shares a <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_New_Zealand" title="Monarchy of New Zealand">head of state</a> with New Zealand as well as having <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_nationality_law" title="New Zealand nationality law">shared citizenship</a>. </td>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="SADR"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a></b> </td> 
 <td style="background:LemonChiffon;"><span style="display:none">D</span> No membership </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Recognised at some stage by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="International recognition of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">84&nbsp;UN member states</a>, 45 of which have since withdrawn or frozen their recognition. It is a founding member of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> and the Asian–African Strategic Partnership formed at the 2005 <a href="/wiki/Asian%E2%80%93African_Conference" class="mw-redirect" title="Asian–African Conference">Asian–African Conference</a>. The territories under its control, the so-called <a href="/wiki/Free_Zone_(region)" title="Free Zone (region)">Free Zone</a>, are claimed in whole by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> as part of its <a href="/wiki/Southern_Provinces" title="Southern Provinces">Southern Provinces</a>. In turn, the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic claims the part of <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a> to the west of the <a href="/wiki/Wall_(Western_Sahara)" class="mw-redirect" title="Wall (Western Sahara)">Moroccan Wall</a> controlled by Morocco. Its government resides in exile in <a href="/wiki/Tindouf" title="Tindouf">Tindouf</a>, <a href="#Algeria">Algeria</a>. </td>
</tr>

 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B </span>Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A <i>de facto</i> independent state,<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[70]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">recognised by</a> Russia, Nicaragua, Nauru, Syria, Venezuela, Abkhazia, Artsakh and Transnistria. Claimed in whole by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Administrative_Entity_of_South_Ossetia" class="mw-redirect" title="Provisional Administrative Entity of South Ossetia">Provisional Administrative Entity of South Ossetia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-cnnAbSO_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnnAbSO-104">[71]</a></sup> </td>

<tr> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Taiwan"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of China<sup id="cite_ref-ChinaTaiwan_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ChinaTaiwan-23">[l]</a></sup> </td> 
 <td style="background:Orchid;"><span style="display:none">D</span> <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">Former UN member</a> and former permanent <a href="/wiki/UN_Security_Council" class="mw-redirect" title="UN Security Council">UN Security Council</a> member (as Republic of China, 1945–1971)<br>Observer in one <a href="/wiki/List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations">UN specialized agency</a> under the name "<a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>" </td> 
 <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> </span>Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a> Claimed by <a href="#Argentina">Argentina</a></span> </td> 
 <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A state competing (nominally) for recognition with the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> (PRC) as the government of China since 1949. The Republic of China (ROC) controls the island of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> and associated islands, Quemoy, Matsu, the Pratas and parts of the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a>, and has not renounced claims over its annexed territories on the <a href="/wiki/Mainland_China" title="Mainland China">mainland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[72]</a></sup> The ROC is recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="International recognition of the Republic of China">14</a> UN member states and the Holy See as of 20 September 2019, none of which recognise the PRC. Additionally, one UN member (<a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a>) has <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Taiwan#Entities_with_no_relations_with_either_ROC_or_PRC" title="Foreign relations of Taiwan">refrained from recognising</a> either the ROC or the PRC. <p>The territory of the ROC is claimed in whole by the PRC.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-24">[m]</a></sup> The ROC <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Taiwan#Relations_with_international_organizations" title="Foreign relations of Taiwan">participates in international organizations</a> under a variety of pseudonyms, most commonly "<a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>" and in the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">WTO</a> it has full membership. The ROC was a founding member of the UN and enjoyed membership from 1945 to 1971, with veto power in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">UN Security Council</a>. See <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">China and the United Nations</a>. </p> </td>
</tr>

 <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Transnistria"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Transnistria_%28state%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a></b>&nbsp;– Pridnestrovian Moldavian Republic </td>
